to receive an email from the System Student Health Insurance Provider (SSHIP), Academic HealthPlans (AHP).  This email will give you the option to either enroll in SSHIP to retrieve an insurance identification card or request an insurance waiver.  \n\nYou may find that some of your friends have already received this email.  Students who were not registered at the time ISS reported registered students for Fall 2013 to AHP, did not receive email communication from AHP.  Please know ISS is updating AHP weekly of those who are registered.\n\nWhen requesting the health insurance waiver, it is important that you include all benefit documents and proof of current enrollment in policy.  If you do not include all benefits and proof of active enrollment, AHP will not be able to verify if your policy meets the requirements and will deny your waiver request.\n\nThe deadline to request the waiver is August 30th.\n\nSincerely,\n\nAmy R.
